[keyterm]

[comments]
Hebrew: חֶסֶד

\f bienveillance

\cme evil, event provoking shame

\cmf mal, evenement qui deshonore

\cme faithfulness of God in keeping the covenant

\cmf fidélité de Dieu selon l'alliance

\cme kindness of person to person in doing favors

\cmf bienveillance des hommes aux hommes

\cme loyalty and faithfulness of a person

\cmf loyauté d'une personne

\cme mercy and kindness given to poor and needy

\cmf pitié donner aux pauvres

\cme mercy of God in forgiveness of sin
